												<div class="c-wysiwyg">
													<h2 id="introduction">Introduction</h2>
<p>In 2021, we began to investigate an attack on the telecom industry in South Asia. During the investigation, we discovered QSC: a multi-plugin malware framework that loads and runs plugins (modules) in memory. The framework includes a Loader, a Core module, a Network module, a Command Shell module and a File Manager module. It is dropped either as a standalone executable or as a payload file along with a loader DLL. In this post, we describe each component of the framework as well as its recent activity including a deployment scenario, an additional backdoor, post-compromise activity and a link to the CloudComputating group.</p>
<h2 id="qsc-framework-components">QSC framework components</h2>
<h3 id="the-loader">The Loader</h3>
<p>The Loader implant is a service DLL with the internal name 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b847937688342" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">loader</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">dll</span></span></span>. It contains the string &#8220;E:\project\test\qt\bin\module\loader\x64\release\loader.pdb&#8221; as its PDB path. The Loader is configured to either read code from 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b84d292346097" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-h">&lt;</span><span class="crayon-i">systemdir</span><span class="crayon-h">&gt;</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">drivers</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">msnet</span></span></span> or read 0x100 (256) bytes from 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b84f983655049" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">n_600s</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">sys</span></span></span>, located in the same directory as the module, to get the file path containing code. If it reads the file path from 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b850553268410" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">n_600s</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">sys</span></span></span>, it deletes the file afterwards. The Loader then reads and decompresses code from the provided file path. It reflectively injects the decompressed code into memory and calls the exported method 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b852084435561" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">plugin_working</span></span></span>. The code injected by the Loader is the Core module, which is described below.</p>
<h2 id="the-core-and-network-modules">The Core and Network modules</h2>
<p>The Core module has an internal name, 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b853868918473" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">qscmdll</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">dll</span></span></span>, and exports only one method, named 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b854725693904" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">plugin_working</span></span></span>. It contains the string &#8220;E:\project\test\qt\bin\module\qscmdll\x64\release\qscmdll.pdb&#8221; as its PDB path. The Loader module passes the file path that contains the compressed Network module code as one of the parameters to the Core module.</p>
<p>The Core module reads the Network module (from the passed file path), decompresses it and injects it into memory. The Network module is a 64-bit DLL with the internal name 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b856830752432" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">qscnetwork</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">dll</span></span></span>. It contains the string &#8220;E:\project\test\qt\bin\module\qscnetwork\x64\release\qscnetwork.pdb&#8221; as its PDB path. The Network module exports the methods 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b857588783401" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">setConfig</span></span></span>, 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b858757629532" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">checkTarget</span></span></span> and 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b859086964004" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">getNetWork</span></span></span>.</p>
<p>The Core module, after injecting the Network module into memory, initializes it by calling its exported methods in sequence:</p>
<ul>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b85a748786909" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">setConfig</span></span></span>: copy configuration data from the Core module to the Network module.</li>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b85b238758502" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">checkTarget</span></span></span>: validate configuration fields by checking that the lengths of the fields are within their size limits.</li>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b85d373906107" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">getNetWork</span></span></span>: prepare and get the network object from the Network module for C2 communication. The Network module uses TLS implementation from the MbedTLS library.</li>
</ul>
<p>In some of the cases, we found that the C2 in the configuration data contained an internal/proxy IP address, which suggested that the attackers were already aware of the target network topology. The configuration file contained the following settings:</p>
<ul>
<li>C2 IP address;</li>
<li>Port;</li>
<li>Sleep time;</li>
<li>Internal/Proxy IP address;</li>
<li>Proxy port;</li>
<li>Proxy username;</li>
<li>Proxy password.</li>
</ul>
<p>The Core module supports the following C2 commands:</p>
<table width="100%">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td width="25%"><strong>Command</strong></td>
<td width="75%"><strong>Description</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>0x1E0001</td>
<td>Send target information (e.g. computer name, user name, OS version, etc.)</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>0x1E0002</td>
<td>XOR decode, decompress and load the Command Shell module bytes into memory.<br />
If the File Manager module is not loaded, then load it before loading the Command Shell module.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>0x1E0003</td>
<td>XOR decode, decompress and load the File Manager module bytes into memory.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>0x1E0004</td>
<td>Heartbeat signal, sent every 2 minutes</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>0x1E0007</td>
<td>Update the code file path. Create 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b85e238521617" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">n_600s</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">sys</span></span></span>, and write 0x100 (256) bytes received from C2 to this file.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h2 id="the-file-manager-module">The File Manager module</h2>
<p>The File Manager module has the internal name 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b85f333658378" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">qscBrowse</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">dll</span></span></span>. It contains the string &#8220;E:\project\test\qt\bin\module\qscBrowse\x64\release\qscBrowse.pdb&#8221; as its PDB path, and exports the following methods.</p>
<ul>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b860181971937" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">destroy</span></span></span>: Free objects relating to network connection, file browsing and file transmission.</li>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b861390547160" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">destroyTransmit</span></span></span>: Free network connection and file transmit operation related objects.</li>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b862942019267" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">startBrowse</span></span></span>: Browse file system.</li>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b863177609917" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">startTransmit</span></span></span>: Read/write file from/to system.</li>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b864907499742" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">stop</span></span></span>: Close network connection. Stop the browsing and transmitting operations.</li>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b866088062755" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">stopTransmit</span></span></span>: Close network connection and stop file transmitting operations.</li>
</ul>
<p>The Core module, after reflectively injecting the File Manager module, calls its 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b867297657894" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">startBrowse</span></span></span> method. The 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b868680227625" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">startTransmit</span></span></span> exported method of the File Manager module contains functionality to read/write files from/to the system. It is called when the module executes certain commands. The File Manager module supports following C2 commands:</p>
<table width="100%">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td width="25%"><strong>Command</strong></td>
<td width="75%"><strong>Description</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>0x0A20010</td>
<td>If the sub-command is 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b869926602107" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-h">&lt;</span><span class="crayon-i">root</span><span class="crayon-h">&gt;</span></span></span>, then get the logical drive letters and types in the system. Otherwise, send a list of files and folders at a specified path.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>0x0A20011</td>
<td>This is similar to the previous command, but it gets a list of files and folders at a specified path with the following properties:</p>
<ul>
<li>LastAccessTime for folders;</li>
<li>LastAccessTime and FileSize for files.</li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>0x0A20012</td>
<td>Read the file and send it to the C2.<br />
This is done by calling the 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b86a643165872" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">startTransmit</span></span></span> method.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>0x0A20013</td>
<td>Create a file in the system and write data from the C2 to the file.<br />
This is done by calling the 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b86b690832131" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">startTransmit</span></span></span> method.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>0x0A20014</td>
<td>Delete a file from the system.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>0x0A20015</td>
<td>Move a file from an existing location to a new one.</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>
<h2 id="command-shell-module">Command Shell module</h2>
<p>The Command Shell module has the internal name 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b86c371485828" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">qscShell</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">dll</span></span></span>. It contains the string &#8220;E:\project\test\qt\bin\module\qscShell\x64\release\qscShell.pdb&#8221; as its PDB path, and exports the methods below.</p>
<ul>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b86e339678262" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">destroy</span></span></span>: Free network connection and command shell related objects.</li>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b86f109573994" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">startShell</span></span></span>: Spawn 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b870770282469" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">cmd</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> as a command shell.</li>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b871315394431" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">stop</span></span></span>: Close the network connection and terminate the command shell process.</li>
</ul>
<p>The Core module, after reflectively injecting the Command Shell module, calls its 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b872667127467" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">startShell</span></span></span> method. The Command Shell module launches 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b873504322430" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-sy">%</span><span class="crayon-i">windir</span><span class="crayon-sy">%</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">system32</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">cmd</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> as a shell using the CreateProcess API, and data is written to and read from the shell using pipes. If the size of the received data exceeds 0xB (11) bytes, it checks if the received data starts with one of the command strings below. If the data does not start with one of these command strings, it is written to the command shell via a pipe.</p>
<p>If there is no more data to receive, the command shell is closed by issuing an 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b874273577423" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">exit</span></span></span> command.</p>
<table width="100%">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td width="40%"><strong>Command</strong></td>
<td width="60%"><strong>Description</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>.put</td>
<td>Create a file and write content to it.<br />
This is done by calling the 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b875415782888" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">startTransmit</span></span></span> method of the File Manager module.</td>
</tr>
<tr>

			<span id="crayon-672e44097b876095577780" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">startTransmit</span></span></span> method of the File Manager module.</td>
</tr>

			<span id="crayon-672e44097b878466883690" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">dest_file</span></span></span> to those of 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b879156106620" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">source_file</span></span></span>.</td>

<h2 id="qsc-framework-and-goclient-backdoor-deployment">QSC framework and GoClient backdoor deployment</h2>
<p>When we first discovered the QSC framework in 2021, we had insufficient telemetry to find out how the framework was deployed or who the threat actor behind it was. We continued to monitor our telemetry for further signs of the QSC framework. In October 2023, we detected multiple instances of QSC files targeting an ISP in West Asia. Our investigation found that the target machines had been infected with the <a href="https://unit42.paloaltonetworks.com/playful-taurus/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Quarian backdoor</a> version 3 (aka Turian) since 2022, and the same attackers had used this access to deploy the QSC framework starting on October 10, 2023.</p>
<p>In addition to the QSC framework, the attackers also deployed a new backdoor written in Golang, which we have named &#8220;GoClient&#8221;. We saw the first deployment of this GoClient backdoor on October 17, 2023. After analyzing all the artifacts from this campaign, we assess, with medium confidence, that the CloudComputating threat actor is behind the deployment of the QSC framework and the GoClient backdoor.</p>
<h3 id="qsc-framework-deployment">QSC framework deployment</h3>
<p>In October 2023, our telemetry showed that the Quarian backdoor was used to copy 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b87a499775933" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">c</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">windows</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">system32</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">cmd</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> to 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b87b728965418" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">c</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">windows</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">task</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> and launch the command shell. The batch script is executed via the command shell.</p>
		<div id="crayon-672e44097b87c774918183" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">

		</div><p>
As can be seen above, a service is created to launch the QSC framework loader DLL 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b87e835777512" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">swprr</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">dll</span></span></span>.</p>
<p>In the same month, our telemetry indicated that yet another batch script had been executed via the Quarian backdoor, with similar commands:</p>
		<div id="crayon-672e44097b87f111120829" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><span class="crayon-title"></span>
			<div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers"><div class="crayon-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code"><div class="crayon-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap"><div class="crayon-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code"><div class="crayon-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy"><div class="crayon-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window"><div class="crayon-button-icon"></div></div></div></div>
			<div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div>
			<div class="crayon-plain-wrap"><textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">

reg add HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE\SYSTEM\CurrentControlSet\services\rasauto\Parameters /v

ping  -n 120 127.0.0.1
net  start rasauto</textarea></div>

class="crayon-cn">127.0.0.1</span></div><div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-672e44097b87f111120829-6"><span class="crayon-e">net&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span class="crayon-e">start </span><span class="crayon-i">rasauto</span></div></div></td>
					</tr>

			</div>
		</div><p>
Just like the previous set of commands, the goal is to create a service to launch the QSC framework loader DLL 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b880047071764" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">rasautosvc</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">dll</span></span></span>.</p>
<p>About a month later, the attacker launched a command shell (
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b881165249248" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">cmd</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span>) using the QSC framework loader DLL file 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b882403583987" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">C</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">Windows</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">System32</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">rasautosvc</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">dll</span></span></span>, and dropped the following multiple QSC framework binaries in the specified order:</p>
<ul>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b883443294764" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">C</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">Windows</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">L2Schemas</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">update</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> (MD5 d99d97bb78929023d77d080da1b10f42)</li>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b884729250416" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">C</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">Windows</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">L2Schemas</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">update</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> (MD5 7f89a83cda93ed3ddaa4315ea4ebba45)</li>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b885148265455" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">C</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">Windows</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">L2Schemas</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">update</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> (MD5 d99d97bb78929023d77d080da1b10f42)</li>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b886955474795" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">C</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">Windows</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">L2Schemas</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">update</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> (MD5 112820e9a87239c2e11ead80759bef85)</li>
<li>
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b888396192964" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">C</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">Windows</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">L2Schemas</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">update</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> (MD5 d99d97bb78929023d77d080da1b10f42)</li>
</ul>
<p>Over the course of the next few months, more QSC framework binaries were dropped on the system via the same mechanism.</p>
<h3 id="goclient-backdoor-deployment">GoClient backdoor deployment</h3>
<p>Also in October 2023, we found that the threat actor dropped and executed the GoClient backdoor file onto the affected system as 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b889224637643" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">c</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">programdata</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">usoshared</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">intop64</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span>, again using the Quarian backdoor infection.</p>
<h4 id="goclient-backdoor">GoClient backdoor</h4>
<p>The GoClient backdoor file communicates with the C2, hardcoded in the malware, via TLS. In order to initiate the communication, the malware prepares the challenge key by base64-encoding the hardcoded value of &#8220;177a7b1cf2441c7ebf626ebc7e807017&#8221; and sending it to the C2 server. If the challenge key is accepted, the C2 server sends a 16-byte value, which will be used as an RC4 key to encrypt/decrypt all subsequent messages between the malware and the server.</p>
<p>Next, the malware collects a list of system information (e.g. hostname, local IP, number of CPUs, etc.) from the victim&#8217;s machine in JSON format, encrypts it with an RC4 key, encodes it in base64 and sends it to the server.</p>
<p>The backdoor then receives a base64-encoded and RC4-encrypted, space-delimited list of command strings from the C2 server to execute on the victim&#8217;s machine.</p>
<p>The main C2 commands available are listed below:</p>
<table width="100%">
<tbody>
<tr>
<td width="25%"><strong>Command</strong></td>
<td width="75%"><strong>Description</strong></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>89562</td>
<td>File manipulation. After checking available disk space on all drives and sending the information back to the C2, the backdoor can receive follow-up commands which can be:</p>
<ul>
<li>717953: Rename file;</li>
<li>789852: Change file time attributes;</li>
<li>7412369: Upload file;</li>
<li>7417862: Download file;</li>
<li>6cb6928f: Remove file.</li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>98423</td>
<td>Command execution. The backdoor requests additional commands from the C2. The follow-up commands below can be received:</p>
<ul>
<li>7412369: Upload file;</li>
<li>7417862: Download file;</li>
<li>79c461a4: Set a variable that holds the character encoding string (the default value is &#8220;UTF-8&#8221;);</li>
<li>cd: Change current working directory;</li>
<li>chdir: Change current working directory;</li>
<li>75391: Close the connection;</li>
<li>Any other command: Create a 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b88a004384958" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">cmd</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span><span class="crayon-h"> </span>/<span class="crayon-i">c</span></span></span> process. Write the received commands to stdin pipe for execution and read the output from stdout pipes.</li>
</ul>
</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>dc191340</td>
<td>Close the connection, delete its own module file and terminate its own process.</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>26c108d6</td>
<td>Create a screenshot of the machine and save on a file named 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b88b562382996" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">cap</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">png</span></span></span>.</td>
</tr>

<h2 id="post-compromise-activity-using-the-goclient-backdoor">Post-compromise activity using the GoClient backdoor</h2>
<p>As mentioned above, the GoClient backdoor can be used to execute commands on a target system. This functionality was frequently used by the attackers. For example, they dropped the legitimate 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b88c596770546" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">rar</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> file in c:\inetpub\temp\ and uploaded a batch script, 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b88e065427627" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-cn">1.bat</span></span></span>, to the same location. Next, according to our telemetry, they executed 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b88f913082413" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-cn">1.bat</span></span></span>. The batch script contains the following commands:</p>
		<div id="crayon-672e44097b890454686428" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">

As can be seen from the list of executed commands, the attackers are primarily interested in collecting system information. Only at the end do they disable UAC remote restrictions and compress the harvested data with the previously uploaded 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b891394958798" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">rar</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> utility.</p>
<h2 id="post-compromise-activity-using-the-qsc-framework">Post-compromise activity using the QSC framework</h2>
<p>The QSC framework was also leveraged to execute a series of commands to find the domain controller on the network, the file server and other machines as shown below. The domain controller was queried to view the list of users within the groups &#8220;domain controllers&#8221; and &#8220;domain computers&#8221;:</p>

The attackers then dropped a tool to c:\Windows\L2Schemas\we.exe. We could not obtain a copy of 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b893876779928" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">we</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span>, but it was used to log in to the domain controller machine using the &#8220;pass the hash&#8221; technique and execute commands remotely:</p>
		<div id="crayon-672e44097b894101319107" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">

Next, the actor tried to list the users under the group &#8220;domain admins&#8221;:</p>

		</div><p>
One of the domain admin accounts was used by the attacker to remotely execute various commands on the domain controller and other machines using WMIC. Commands were executed to obtain the network configuration, and a shadow copy of the C: drive and the NTDS database. All information thus collected was then stored at user\downloads\1.txt on the domain controller:</p>
		<div id="crayon-672e44097b897222881832" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">

		</div><p>
<h2 id="lateral-movement-deploying-the-qsc-framework">Lateral movement (deploying the QSC framework)</h2>
<p>By using WMIC and the stolen domain admin credentials, the attackers were able to execute the QSC framework on other machines within the affected network. We found multiple instances during our investigation where the attackers used WMIC to remotely run either a QSC framework loader DLL or a QSC framework executable on a target machine.</p>
<p>We found that the QSC framework sample 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b898487720667" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">update</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> (MD5 d99d97bb78929023d77d080da1b10f42) was configured to use a local IP address (pivot machine address 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b899060934827" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-cn">172.17.99</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-cn">5</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-cn">8080</span></span></span>) as a C2 address. Similarly, the sample 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b89a049909096" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">update</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> (MD5 7f89a83cda93ed3ddaa4315ea4ebba45) was configured to use an internal IP address (pivot machine address 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b89b901945361" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-cn">172.17.99</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-cn">5</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-cn">80</span></span></span>) but run on port 80. This might suggest either that these samples were deployed on machines without internet access or that the threat actor decided to channel all C2 communication through selected machines for other reasons.</p>
<p>Just after executing each instance of the above QSC framework samples on the remote machine, the attacker executed 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b89d252751142" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-sy">%</span><span class="crayon-i">windir</span><span class="crayon-sy">%</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">l2schemas</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">pf</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> on the pivot machine. While we could not obtain a copy of 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b89e292831480" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">pf</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span>, it seemed to perform port forwarding operations to forward any traffic coming to the pivot machine&#8217;s local IP address on port 8080/80 to the remote C2 server address 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b89f500807488" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-cn">108.61.206</span><span class="crayon-sy">[</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-sy">]</span><span class="crayon-cn">206</span></span></span> on port 8080.</p>
		<div id="crayon-672e44097b8a0903997899" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
		
			<div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><span class="crayon-title"></span>
			<div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;"><span class="crayon-mixed-highlight" title="Contains Mixed Languages"></span><div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers"><div class="crayon-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code"><div class="crayon-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap"><div class="crayon-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code"><div class="crayon-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy"><div class="crayon-button-icon"></div></div><div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window"><div class="crayon-button-icon"></div></div></div></div>
			<div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div>

<h2 id="attribution">Attribution</h2>
<p>We found multiple artifacts that helped us in attributing the QSC framework and the activity described above to the CloudComputating (aka BackdoorDiplomacy, Faking Dragon) group:</p>
<ul>
<li>On February 23, 2024, our product detected the presence of the file 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b8a2965663676" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">C</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">Windows</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">SysWOW64</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">appmgmt</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">dll</span></span></span> (MD5 97b0a8e8d125e71d3d1dd8e241d70c5b). This DLL file is Quarian backdoor version 3 (aka Turian), compiled on Thursday, 28.04.2022 02:59:40 UTC. Quarian backdoor version 3 (aka Turian) was used to deploy the QSC framework and GoClient backdoor as described above.</li>
<li>The Quarian backdoor sample 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b8a3912529090" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">C</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">Windows</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">SysWOW64</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">appmgmt</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">dll</span></span></span> (MD5 97b0a8e8d125e71d3d1dd8e241d70c5b) was configured to use the domain &#8220;proxy.oracleapps[.]org&#8221;, which was previously used by BackdoorDiplomacy as reported by Bitdefender in their report, &#8220;<a href="https://www.bitdefender.com/files/News/CaseStudies/study/426/Bitdefender-PR-Whitepaper-BackdoorDiplomacy-creat6507-en-EN.pdf" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Cyber-Espionage in the Middle East: Investigating a New BackdoorDiplomacy Threat Actor Campaign</a>&#8220;.</li>
<li>The Quarian backdoor sample code is protected by VMProtect. After unpacking it, our KTAE (Kaspersky Threat Attribution Engine) attribution engine found a high degree of similarity with the CloudComputating group&#8217;s other malware.
<div id="attachment_114441" style="width: 948px" class="wp-caption aligncenter"><a href="https://media.kasperskycontenthub.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/43/2024/11/02131624/QSC_framework.png" class="magnificImage"><img loading="lazy" decoding="async" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-114441" class="size-full wp-image-114441" src="https://media.kasperskycontenthub.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/43/2024/11/02131624/QSC_framework.png" alt="Kaspersky Threat Attribution Engine analysis" width="938" height="115" srcset="https://media.kasperskycontenthub.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/43/2024/11/02131624/QSC_framework.png 938w, https://media.kasperskycontenthub.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/43/2024/11/02131624/QSC_framework-300x37.png 300w, https://media.kasperskycontenthub.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/43/2024/11/02131624/QSC_framework-768x94.png 768w, https://media.kasperskycontenthub.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/43/2024/11/02131624/QSC_framework-740x91.png 740w, https://media.kasperskycontenthub.com/wp-content/uploads/sites/43/2024/11/02131624/QSC_framework-800x98.png 800w" sizes="(max-width: 938px) 100vw, 938px" /></a><p id="caption-attachment-114441" class="wp-caption-text">Kaspersky Threat Attribution Engine analysis</p></div></li>
<li>We observed that the Quarian backdoor V3 sample 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b8a9380915412" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">C</span><span class="crayon-sy">:</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">Windows</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">SysWOW64</span><span class="crayon-sy">\</span><span class="crayon-i">appmgmt</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">dll</span></span></span> (MD5 97b0a8e8d125e71d3d1dd8e241d70c5b) shell command created a copy of 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b8aa279529057" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">cmd</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> in the Windows directory with 
			<span id="crayon-672e44097b8ab606604012" class="crayon-syntax crayon-syntax-inline  crayon-theme-classic crayon-theme-classic-inline crayon-font-monaco" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important;"><span class="crayon-pre crayon-code" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;font-size: 12px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;"><span class="crayon-i">task</span><span class="crayon-sy">.</span><span class="crayon-i">exe</span></span></span> as the filename.</li>
<li>In this campaign, we found C:\ProgramData\USOShared\ to be a common directory which contained the QSC framework, the GoClient backdoor, Quarian backdoor version 3 binaries and tools used in reconnaissance and post-compromise activity. This also helps in tracing all the implants and tools to the CloudComputating group. Some of the tools, such as TailorScan and StowProxy, are known to have been used by CloudComputating in past activity discovered in the Middle East.<br />

<h2 id="conclusions">Conclusions</h2>
<p>Our investigation has revealed a significant shift in the tactics of the CloudComputating group, marked by their adoption of the QSC framework alongside the previously identified Quarian backdoor and its variants. Our telemetry data indicates that the group has initiated limited yet targeted campaigns using QSC framework and focusing specifically on the telecommunication sector. Additionally, in response to detection of the Quarian backdoor, the group has begun deploying a protected version. The usage of the QSC framework suggests a strategic change in their toolkit, serving as a secondary means to maintain access within compromised networks. This evolution underscores the group&#8217;s adaptability and emphasizes the importance of continuous monitoring of its future activities.</p>
<p>QSC is a modular framework, of which only the initial loader remains on disk while the core and network modules are always in memory. Using a plugin-based architecture gives attackers the ability to control which plugin (module) to load in memory on demand depending on the target of interest.</p>
<h2 id="iocs">IOCs</h2>
<p><strong>QSC framework Loader</strong><br />
<a href="https://opentip.kaspersky.com/d88ef85941ec6be99fd1e38ad5702bae/?icid=gl_OpenTIP_acq_ona_smm__onl_b2b_securelist_lnk_sm-team_______e0415539b98075bf&amp;utm_source=SL&amp;utm_medium=SL&amp;utm_campaign=SL" target="_blank" rel="noopener">d88ef85941ec6be99fd1e38ad5702bae</a><br />

<a href="https://opentip.kaspersky.com/97b0a8e8d125e71d3d1dd8e241d70c5b/?icid=gl_OpenTIP_acq_ona_smm__onl_b2b_securelist_lnk_sm-team_______626409aeab0b0d7d&amp;utm_source=SL&amp;utm_medium=SL&amp;utm_campaign=SL" target="_blank" rel="noopener">97b0a8e8d125e71d3d1dd8e241d70c5b</a><br />

			<h3 class="c-card__title"><a  data-element-id="footer-reports-title"   href="https://securelist.com/eastwind-apt-campaign/113345/" class="c-card__link">EastWind campaign: new CloudSorcerer attacks on government organizations in Russia</a></h3>		</header>
				<div class="c-card__desc u-hidden u-block@md">

		</div>
